###Intro###
country_event = {
	id = tram.intro
	immediate = { 
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.intro"
		hidden_effect = {
			activate_mission = TRM_visit_from_japan
			activate_mission = TRM_nra_sabotage
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = ENT decision = TRM_Seek_For_Entente_Support }
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 505058 }
				unit_leader_event = { id = tram.2 days = 646 random_days = 100 }
				unit_leader_event = { id = tram.3 days = 646 random_days = 100 }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = tram_crisis_1936.1
					days = 85
					random_days = 35
				}
				country_event = {
					id = tram_crisis_1936.3
					days = 130
					random_days = 35
				}
				country_event = {
					id = tram_crisis_1936.4
					days = 170
					random_days = 35
				}
				country_event = {
					id = tram_crisis_1936.5
					days = 245
					random_days = 35
				}
				RUS = {
					country_event = {
						id = tram_crisis_1937.1
						days = 285
						random_days = 15
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	title = tram.intro.t
	desc = tram.intro.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = tram.intro.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = trammlad.147
				days = 10
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.intro.b
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		country_event = tram.999
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = trammlad.147
				days = 10
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = tram.994001
	immediate = {
		annex_country = { target = SIB transfer_troops = yes }
	}
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = TRM
		has_country_leader = {
			name = "Ivan Lavrov"
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		SIB = {
			exists = yes
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Ivan Lavrov"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 } 
	fire_only_once = yes
}

###Transamur breaks away###

country_event = { #Transamur breaks away!
	id = tram.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.1" }
	title = tram.1.t
	desc = tram.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #war
		name = tram.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		set_global_flag = PRI_breaksaway
		hidden_effect = {
			TRM = {
				TRM_remove_japanese_influence = yes
			}
			JAP = {
				remove_from_faction = TRM
				if = {
					limit = { has_war_with = RUS }
					RUS = { save_event_target_as = white_peace_receiver }
					white_peace_with_TARGET = yes
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = TRM
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #leave them
		name = tram.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		set_global_flag = PRI_breaksaway
		add_stability = -0.15
		hidden_effect = {
			TRM = {
				TRM_remove_japanese_influence = yes
				separate_peace_all_wars = yes
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			remove_from_faction = TRM
		}
	}
}
unit_leader_event = { #Diterikhs dies
	id = tram.2
	title = tram.2.t
	desc = tram.2.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		ROOT = { TRM_do_rovs_in_power = yes }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = tram.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		ROOT = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_unit_leader = 505058
				}
				random_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 505058 }			
					remove_unit_leader = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						ruling_only = yes
						name = "Mikhail Diterikhs"
					}
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Vladimir Kappel"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_RUS_Vladimir_Kappel.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = junta_subtype
				}
			}
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 505060 }
				promote_leader = yes
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
			add_ideas = TRM_Vladimir_Kappel_hog_pau  
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.2.b
		trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Nikita I"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				has_idea = TRM_Spiridon_Merkulov_eco_sco
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		ROOT = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_unit_leader = 505058
				}
				random_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 505058 }			
					remove_unit_leader = yes
				}
			}
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 505060 }
				promote_leader = yes
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
			add_ideas = TRM_Nikolay_Merkulov_hog_sco  
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.2.c
		trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Nikita I"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				has_idea = TRM_Vladimir_Gantimurov_sec_ade
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		ROOT = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_unit_leader = 505058
				}
				random_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 505058 }			
					remove_unit_leader = yes
				}
			}
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 505060 }
				promote_leader = yes
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
			add_ideas = TRM_Vladimir_Gantimurov_hog_ade  
		}
		set_country_flag = Mikhail_Diterikhs_dead
	}
}
unit_leader_event = { #Diterikhs dies
	id = tram.3
	immediate = { set_country_flag = Mikhail_Diterikhs_dead }
	title = tram.2.t
	desc = tram.3.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		ROOT = { 
			TRM_do_rovs_in_power = no
			NOT = { has_country_flag = Mikhail_Diterikhs_dead }
		}		
	}	
	option = {
		name = tram.3.a
		ROOT = {
			add_political_power = 25
			add_stability = -0.01
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_unit_leader = 505058
				}
				random_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 505058 }			
					remove_unit_leader = yes
				}
			}
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 505060 }
				promote_leader = yes
			}	
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Kirill dies
	id = tram.5
	title = {
		text = rusd.95.t.tsar
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = TRM_Monarchy
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = rusd.95.t.other
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = TRM_Monarchy }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rusd.95.d.tsar
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				ruling_only = yes
				name = "Kirill I"
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rusd.95.d.other
		trigger = {
			NOT = { 
				has_country_leader = {
					ruling_only = yes
					name = "Kirill I"
				} 
			}
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = TRM
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = rusd.95.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				ruling_only = yes
				name = "Kirill I"
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = Kirill_Romanov_dead
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Vladimir III"
			desc = "POLITICS_VLADIMIR_ROMANOV_ABS_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_RUS_Vladimir_Romanov.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = absolute_monarchy_subtype
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rusd.95.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { 
				has_country_leader = {
					ruling_only = yes
					name = "Kirill I"
				} 
			}
		}	
		add_political_power = -15
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = tram.10
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.10" }
	title = tram.10.t
	desc = tram.10.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = tram.10.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_idea = TRM_oblastniki_influence_idea }
			}
			add_ideas = TRM_oblastniki_influence_idea
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TRM_oblastniki_influence_idea
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TRM_oblastniki_influence_idea
				add_idea = TRM_OBL_INF_1
			}
		}
	}
}
### Amur Railway
country_event = {
	id = tram.11
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.11" }
	title = tram.11.t
	desc = tram.11.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = tram.11.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
		}
		trigger = {
			TRM_JAP_not_hostile = yes
			has_socialist_government = no
		}
		JAP = {
			country_event = {
				id = tram.12
				days = 2
				random_days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.11.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = TRM_entente_full_support
				has_country_flag = TRM_entente_partial_support
			}
			has_socialist_government = no
		}
		CAN = {
			country_event = {
				id = tram.12
				days = 2
				random_days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.11.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
		}
		trigger = {
			country_exists = USA
			USA = { has_war = no }
			has_socialist_government = no
		}
		USA = {
			country_event = {
				id = tram.12
				days = 2
				random_days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.11.e
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
		}
		set_country_flag = TRM_build_the_bam_railway_completed
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = TRM_build_the_bam_railway_1 }
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = TRM_build_the_bam_railway_2 }
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = TRM_build_the_bam_railway_3 }
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = TRM_build_the_bam_railway_4 }
		set_variable = { TRM_bam_railway_cost = 50 }
		set_variable = { TRM_bam_railway_duration = 100 }
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = tram.12
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.12" }
	title = tram.12.t
	desc = tram.12.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = tram.12.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				tag = JAP
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				tag = CAN
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_stability < 0
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = tram.14
				days = 2
				random_days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.12.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.3
				tag = JAP
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.4
				tag = CAN
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				has_stability < 0
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = tram.15
				days = 2
				random_days = 5
			}
		}	
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = tram.14
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.14" }
	title = tram.14.t
	desc = tram.14.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = tram.14.a
		set_country_flag = TRM_build_the_bam_railway_completed
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = TRM_build_the_bam_railway_1 }
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = TRM_build_the_bam_railway_2 }
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = TRM_build_the_bam_railway_3 }
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = TRM_build_the_bam_railway_4 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { tag = JAP }
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = 0.02
			}
			set_variable = { TRM_bam_railway_cost = 30 }
			set_variable = { TRM_bam_railway_duration = 60 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { gives_military_access_to = FROM }
				}
				give_military_access = FROM
			}
			set_country_flag = TRM_japanese_railways
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { tag = CAN }
			}
			set_variable = { TRM_bam_railway_cost = 40 }
			set_variable = { TRM_bam_railway_duration = 70 }
			set_country_flag = TRM_canadian_railways
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { tag = USA }
			}
			set_variable = { TRM_bam_railway_cost = 25 }
			set_variable = { TRM_bam_railway_duration = 65 }
			set_country_flag = TRM_american_railways
		}		
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_approves_of_govt
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = tram.24
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.24" }
	title = tram.24.t
	desc = tram.24.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = tram.24.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = RUS
			type = annex_everything
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = {
				id = russianews.7
				days = 1
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tag = RUS }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = russianews.7
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.24.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		RUS = {
			transfer_state = 565
			transfer_state = 563
			transfer_state = 564
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
				has_country_flag = TRM_oblastniki_operate
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.15
			}
		}
	}
}
###Soviets transfer states###
country_event = {
	id = tram.25
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.25" }
	title = tram.25.t
	desc = tram.25.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = tram.25.a
		TRM = {
			transfer_state = 566
			566 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			transfer_state = 644
			644 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			transfer_state = 1202
			1202 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = TRM_control_FE
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = JAP
			}
			JAP = {
				country_event = {
					id = tram.42
					days = 7
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Japanese demands Okhotsk and Kamchatka
	id = tram.47
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.47" }
	title = tram.47.t
	desc = tram.47.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		ai_chance = { # Transfer states
			factor = 70
		}
		name = tram.47.a
		JAP = {
			add_state_claim = 637
			transfer_state = 637
			add_state_claim = 562
			transfer_state = 562
		}
	}
	option = { #Break away
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		name = tram.47.b
		JAP = {
			end_puppet = TRM
		}
		JAP = {
			country_event = {
				id = tram.1
				days = 1
			}
		}

country_event = { #
	id = tram.73
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.73" }
	title = tram.73.t
	desc = tram.73.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = tram.73.a
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				has_government = social_liberal
				AND = {
					has_government = social_democrat
					has_cosmetic_tag = TRM_SIB
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 60 }
		add_stability = 0.1
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_10 = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = social_liberal }
			set_cosmetic_tag = TRM_SIB_usa
		}
	}	
}



####Political####
###Anti-Kolchak Coup###
country_event = {
	id = tram.80
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.80" }
	title = tram.80.t
	desc = tram.80.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #Kolchak survived
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_MONARCHY }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_OBLASTNIKI }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_SEMYONOV }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_SEMYONOV_MONARCHY }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_SEMYONOV_REPUBLIC }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_YUI }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_SOCDEM_MLADOROSSI}
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_MLADOROSSI }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_NATSI }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_PEPEL }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_PEPEL_OBL }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_KOLCHAK_SECURES_POWER }
			}			
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { TRM_Overall_Kolchak_Support > 0.3 }
				AND = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_KOLCHAK_SECURES_POWER }
					is_ai = yes
				}
			}
		}
		name = tram.80.a
		add_stability = -0.25
		set_country_flag = TRM_Kolchak_alive
		remove_country_leader_trait = TRM_shaky_rule
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				news_event = {
					id = tramnews.2
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Kolchak survived with Japanese help
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_MONARCHY }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_OBLASTNIKI }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_SEMYONOV }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_SEMYONOV_MONARCHY }					
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_SEMYONOV_REPUBLIC }					
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_YUI }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_SOCDEM_MLADOROSSI}
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_MLADOROSSI }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_NATSI }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_PEPEL }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_PEPEL_OBL }
				}
			}
		}
		name = tram.80.b
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat > 0.24 }
		}
		set_country_flag = TRM_Kolchak_alive
		remove_country_leader_trait = TRM_shaky_rule
		add_stability = -0.3
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		get_current_government_type = yes
		JAP = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = TRM
				autonomous_state = kr_occupied_puppet
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			restore_previous_government_type = yes
			random_other_country = {
				news_event = {
					id = tramnews.2
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Kolchak dead
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_KOLCHAK_SECURES_POWER }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_SEMYONOV }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_SEMYONOV_MONARCHY }					
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_SEMYONOV_REPUBLIC }					
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { ROVSOrientation < 0.99 }
				check_variable = { CossackOrientation < 0.99 }
				AND = {
					is_ai = yes
					OR = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_MONARCHY }
						has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_OBLASTNIKI }
						has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_SEMYONOV }
						has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_SEMYONOV_MONARCHY }					
						has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_SEMYONOV_REPUBLIC }					
						has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_YUI }
						has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_SOCDEM_MLADOROSSI}
						has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_MLADOROSSI }
						has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_NATSI }
						has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_PEPEL }
						has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_PEPEL_OBL }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = tram.80.c
		country_event = tram.81
		add_stability = -0.4		
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Mikhail Diterikhs"
			desc = "POLITICS_DITERIKHS_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/TRM/Portrait_TRM_Diterikhs.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = junta_subtype
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			long_name = TRM_rovs_party_long
			name = TRM_rovs_party
		}
		set_country_flag = Aleksandr_Kolchak_dead
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				news_event = {
					id = tramnews.1
					days = 1
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = TRM_Aleksandr_Kolchak_cnav_pau
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 50001 }			
				set_nationality = NSW
			}
		}
	}
}

###Kolchak dead, choose new ruler###
country_event = {
	id = tram.81
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.81" }
	title = tram.81.t
	desc = tram.81.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	picture = GFX_news_event_TRM_kolchak_coup

	option = { #New Dictator
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { ROVSOrientation < 0.99 }
				AND = {
					is_ai = yes
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_MONARCHY }
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_MONARCHY }
			}
		}
		name = tram.81.a
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_ideas = TRM_martial_law
		remove_country_leader_trait = TRM_shaky_rule
		if = {
			limit = { TRM_has_japanese_influence = yes }
			JAP = {
				country_event = {
					id = tram.98
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		complete_national_focus = TRM_The_New_Supreme_Ruler
		add_ideas = TRM_Mikhail_K_Diterikhs_hog_pau 
		add_ideas = TRM_Tikhon_Shalamov_for_pau 
		add_ideas = TRM_Dmitriy_Lebedev_eco_pau 
		add_ideas = TRM_Arkady_Udintsev_sec_pau		
	}

	option = {
		name = tram.81.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { CossackOrientation < 0.99 }
				AND = {
					is_ai = yes
					OR = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_SEMYONOV }
						has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_SEMYONOV_MONARCHY }
						has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_SEMYONOV_REPUBLIC }
					}
				}
			}
		}		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_SEMYONOV }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_SEMYONOV_MONARCHY }		
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_SEMYONOV_REPUBLIC }		
				}
			}
		}
		complete_national_focus = TRM_Semyonov_In_Power
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Grigory Semyonov"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/TRM/Portrait_TRM_Grigory_Semyonov.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = pataut_cossack_subtype
			traits = {}
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			long_name = TRM_semyonov_party_long
			name = TRM_semyonov_party
		}
		if = {
			limit = { TRM_has_japanese_influence = yes }
			JAP = {
				country_event = {
					id = tram.98
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tag = TRM }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = tramnews.6
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		set_capital = { state = 563 }
		add_ideas = TRM_Grigoriy_M_Semyenov_hog_pau
		add_ideas = BRT_Ivan_P_Kalmykov_for_pau
		add_ideas = BRT_Leonid_V_Verigo_eco_pau
		add_ideas = TRM_Boris_Shepunov_sec_pau		
	}	
	option = {
		name = tram.81.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_PEPEL }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_PEPEL_OBL }
				}
			}
		}
		complete_national_focus = TRM_Siberian_Suvorov_Regime
		set_cosmetic_tag = TRM_PEPEL
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Anatoliy Pepelyaev"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/TRM/Portrait_TRM_Pepelyaev.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = junta_subtype
		}
		random_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_id = 505060 }
			promote_leader = yes
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = TRM_Anatoliy_Pepelyaev_hog_pau
		add_ideas = TRM_Viktor_N_Pepelyayev_for_mli
		add_ideas = TRM_Anatoliy_Pepelyaev_eco_pau
		add_ideas = TRM_Georgiy_Stark_sec_sco
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			long_name = TRM_pepelyaev_party_long
			name = TRM_pepelyaev_party
		}
		if = {
			limit = { TRM_has_japanese_influence = yes }
			JAP = {
				country_event = {
					id = tram.98
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = tram.10005
				days = 2
			}
		}			
	}	
	option = {
		name = tram.81.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_SOCDEM_MLADOROSSI}
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_MLADOROSSI }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_NATSI }
				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		
		set_country_flag = TRM_Mlad_in_power

		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = TRM_Alexander_Kazembek_hog_tot
		add_ideas = TRM_Sergey_Obolensky_for_tot
		add_ideas = TRM_Vladimir_Merzheevsky_eco_tot
		add_ideas = TRM_Vladimir_Krasinskiy_sec_tot
		set_cosmetic_tag = TRM_Mlad
			
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = TRM_Aleksandr_Kolchak_cnav_pau
			hidden_effect = {
				random_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 50001 }			
					set_nationality = NSW
				}
			}
		}
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			unlock_national_focus = TRM_tsar_soviets
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			complete_national_focus = TRM_tsar_soviets
		}		
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.81.f
		trigger = { has_idea = TRM_Viktor_N_Pepelyayev_hog_mli }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_OBLASTNIKI}
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_MERKULOV }
				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = market_liberal
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = TRM_Aleksandr_Kolchak_cnav_pau
			hidden_effect = {
				random_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 50001 }			
					set_nationality = NSW
				}
			}
		}
		
		effect_tooltip = {
			unlock_national_focus = TRM_Democracy_In_Transamur
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			complete_national_focus = TRM_Democracy_In_Transamur
		}		
	}	
}
###Elections - First Time###
country_event = {
	id = tram.86
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.86" }
	title = tram.86.t
	desc = tram.86.d

	trigger = {
		has_elected_government = yes
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # VKKE
		name = tram.86.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
		}
		add_political_power = -40
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_democrat
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = TRM_Florian_Fedorovich_hog_sde 
		add_ideas = TRM_Mikhail_B_Shatila_for_sde 
		add_ideas = TRM_Vladimir_M_Krutovsky_eco_sde
		add_ideas = TRM_Alexander_E_Novoselov_sec_sde
	}

	option = { # Regionalists

			base = 20
		}

		}

		add_ideas = TRM_Leonid_A_Ustrugov_sec_mli
	}

	option = { # NDS
		name = tram.86.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = TRM_cw_oblastnik_victory }
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_conservative
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
		add_political_power = -40
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.3
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes

		add_ideas = TRM_Tikhon_Shalamov_for_pau 
		add_ideas = TRM_Innokentiy_Tolmachev_eco_sco
		add_ideas = TRM_Georgiy_Stark_sec_sco
	}

	option = { # Military Coup
		name = tram.86.e
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0

###Elections###
country_event = {
	id = tram.87
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.87" }
	title = tram.87.t
	desc = tram.87.d
	trigger = {
		TRM_democrats_in_power = yes
		NOT = {
		TRM_nra_in_power = yes
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # VKKE
		name = tram.86.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
		}
		add_political_power = -40
		clr_country_flag = TRM_oblastniki_operate
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.3
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = TRM_Florian_Fedorovich_hog_sde 
		add_ideas = TRM_Mikhail_B_Shatila_for_sde 
		add_ideas = TRM_Vladimir_M_Krutovsky_eco_sde
		add_ideas = TRM_Alexander_E_Novoselov_sec_sde
		country_event = {
			id = tram.87
			days = 1460
			} #Will fire another election 4 years later
	}

	option = { # KDV
		name = tram.86.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = market_liberal
		}

		date > 1940.1.1
		is_subject_of = JAP

		}

		}

				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = TRM
					relation = guarantee
					active = no
				}
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = TRM
					relation = non_aggression_pact
					active = no
				}
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = TRM

					active = no
				}

					country = TRM

					active = no
				}	
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			remove_from_faction = TRM

			target = TRM

		}

					country = TRM

					active = no
				}

					country = TRM

		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = tram.109
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.109" }
	title = tram.109.t
	desc = tram.109.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_war_with = RUS
	}

	option = { #Accept the deal
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				owns_state = 566
			}
		}
		name = tram.109.a
		add_political_power = 40
		RUS = {
			white_peace_with_ROOT = yes
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = TRM
						state = 565
						state = 566
						state = 575
						state = 564
						state = 563
					}
				}
				TRM = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			country_event = tram.110
		}
		567 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = TRM
					}
					NOT = {
						is_claimed_by = TRM
					}
				}
				add_claim_by = TRM
			}
		}

		set_country_flag = TRM_control_FE
	}

	option = { #Refuse the deal
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		name = tram.109.b
		add_political_power = -20
		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = tram.111
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

###Japanese delegation trying to owerthrow you###
country_event = {
	id = tram.119
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.119" }
	title = tram.119.t
	desc = tram.119.d

	trigger = {
		tag = TRM
		check_variable = { party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat > 0.34 }
		TRM_has_japanese_influence = yes
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				TRM_japanese_in_power = yes
				has_idea = TRM_Grigoriy_M_Semyenov_hog_pau
				TRM_semyenov_in_power = yes
				has_war = yes
			}
			has_country_flag = TRM_delegation_bypass
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}

	option = { #Yui Mitsue owerthrow current government

	id = tram.123
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.123" }
	title = tram.123.t
	desc = tram.123.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = tram.123.a

		custom_effect_tooltip = TRM_agitation_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				15 = {
					set_country_flag = TRM_good_agitation
				}

				40 = {
					set_country_flag = TRM_agitation
				}

				45 = {
					set_country_flag = TRM_bad_agitation
				}
			}
			country_event = tram.124
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		set_country_flag = TRM_no_agitation
		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_increase_chance_of_war
		add_to_variable = { global.siberian_war_chance = 0.01 }
	}

	option = {
		name = tram.123.b
		set_country_flag = TRM_no_agitation
		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_decrease_chance_of_war
		add_to_variable = { global.siberian_war_chance = -0.05 }
	}
}

	id = tram.1004
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.1004" }
	title = tram.1004.t
	desc = tram.1004.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = tram.1004.a #We can't do anything about it
		add_stability = -0.05
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 80
				surrender_progress < 0.05
				GER = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
					OR = {
						has_war_with = FRA
						has_war_with = CAN
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = tram.1004.b #We will at least embargo them!

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				surrender_progress < 0.05
				GER = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
					OR = {
						has_war_with = FRA
						has_war_with = CAN
					}
				}
			}
		}

		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = TRM
			modifier = embargo
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = TRM
				modifier = embargo
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = tram.1004.c #We can beat them again

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				surrender_progress < 0.05
				GER = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
					OR = {
						has_war_with = FRA
						has_war_with = CAN
					}
				}
			}
		}

		add_stability = 0.05

		declare_war_on = {
			target = TRM
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
}

					active = no

country_event = { #Legion
	id = tramczech.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tramczech.1" }
	title = tramczech.1.t
	desc = tramczech.1.d
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = tramczech.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_NRA_COUP }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_NRA_COUP_RADSOC }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_OBLASTNIKI }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_PEPEL }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_PEPEL_OBL }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_SOCDEM_MLADOROSSI }
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		add_stability = -0.15
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = 10000
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = artillery_equipment
			amount = 300
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = support_equipment
			amount = 400
		}	
		delete_unit_template_and_units = {
			division_template = "Chekhoslovatskiy Korpus"
			disband = yes
		}		
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = TRM_Ensure_Czech_Legion_Loyalty }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "No Step Back"
				}
				create_railway_gun = {
					equipment = railway_gun_equipment_1
				}
				create_railway_gun = {
					equipment = railway_gun_equipment_1
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "No Step Back"
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = train_equipment_3
					amount = 3
					producer = TRM
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_tech = railway_gun }
					}
					set_technology = { railway_gun = 1 }
				}
				else = {
					add_tech_bonus = {

country_event = {
	id = tram.309
	title = tram.309.t
	desc = tram.309.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = tram.309.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_stability < 0.2
			}
			add_stability = 0.3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_stability < 0.3
				has_stability > 0.2
			}
			add_stability = 0.25
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_stability < 0.4
				has_stability > 0.3
			}
			add_stability = 0.2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_stability < 0.5
				has_stability > 0.4
			}
			add_stability = 0.15
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_support < 0.5
			}
			add_war_support = 0.15
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_stability < 0.6
				has_stability > 0.5
			}
			add_stability = 0.1
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_stability < 0.7
				has_stability > 0.6
			}
			add_stability = 0.05
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_stability > 0.7
				has_stability < 1
			}
			add_stability = 0.05
		}
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_20 = yes
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_siberia = yes
				NOT = { is_core_of = TRM }
				OR = {
					is_core_of = SOV
					is_core_of = RUS
				}
			}
			TRM = { add_state_core = PREV }
		}
	}
}

			remove_claim_by = ROOT
		}
	}
	title = tram.400.t
	desc = tram.400.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = SOV
			tag = RUS
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = SOV_restored_in_transamur }
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.400.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = TRM
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = TRM
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = TRM }
		if = {
			limit = {
				TRM = { has_socialist_government = no }
				ROOT = { has_socialist_government = no }
			}
			country_event = {
				id = tram.401
				days = 5
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				TRM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = Aleksandr_Kolchak_dead } }
			}
			country_event = {
				id = tram.404
				days = 6
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = rusfor.1208
			days = 2
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.400.b
		trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				OR = {
					has_socialist_government = yes
					has_government = social_democrat
					has_government = social_liberal
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = TRM
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						state = 1246
						state = 408
						state = 409
						state = 560
						state = 561
						state = 657
					}
				}
			}
			add_core_of = ROOT
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 1246
					state = 408
					state = 409
					state = 560
					state = 561
					state = 657
				}
			}
			TRM = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		ROOT = { puppet = TRM }
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					has_socialist_government = yes
				}
			}
			TRM = {
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = totalist
					popularity = 30
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = syndicalist
					popularity = 15
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = radical_socialist
					popularity = 30
				}
													remove_ideas = TRM_dream
				set_cosmetic_tag = TRM_SOV
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					OR = {
						has_government = social_democrat
						has_government = social_liberal
					}
				}
			}
			TRM = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_democrat
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = social_democrat
					popularity = 30
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = social_liberal
					popularity = 15
				}
													remove_ideas = TRM_dream
			}
		}
	}

						ideology = market_liberal

				}
			}
		}

					ideology = market_liberal
					popularity = 15
				}
				random_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 1103 }

					target = MAN
					size = 0.24

				}
			}
		}

			target = MAN
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}

			base = 15

				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TRM_cossack_host_modifier }
			}
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TRM_martial_law_modifier } 
		}
		TRM_clamp_spheres_of_influence = yes
		TRM_recalculate_kolchak_variables = yes
		hidden_effect = { country_event = tram.10003 }
	}	
}
